architecture for trait method resolution and error reporting. **Candidate Collection** happens at two main levels:\\n\\n1. **Trait Candidate Assembly** (compiler/rustc_trait_selection/src/traits/select/candidate_assembly.rs): The `assemble_candidates` function is the primary entry point that examines in-scope trait implementations and assembles a list of candidates for trait obligation resolution.\\n\\n2. **Method Candidate Probing** (compiler/rustc_hir_typeck/src/method/probe.rs): When resolving method calls on a receiver type, the probe module uses `probe_for_name` and `probe_for_name_many` to gather method candidates from inherent implementations and trait extensions. The `pick_all_method` function iterates through autoderef steps to find applicable methods, and `consider_candidates` filters these candidates and returns either a unique pick or an ambiguity error. When multiple candidates are equally valid, `consider_candidates` (line 1727-1741) creates `MethodError::Ambiguity` by collecting the candidate sources.\\n\\n3. **Associated Item Candidate Collection** (compiler/rustc_hir_analysis/src/hir_ty_lowering/mod.rs): The `probe_single_bound_for_assoc_item` function searches for associated items (types, methods, constants) within trait bounds and reports ambiguity when multiple matching bounds define the same item (E0221).\\n\\n**Ambiguous Method Error Reporting** uses three integrated systems:\\n\\n1. **Associated Item Ambiguity** (compiler/rustc_hir_analysis/src/hir_ty_lowering/mod.rs, lines 1121-1200): When `probe_single_bound_for_assoc_item` finds multiple matching candidates, it directly reports an `AmbiguousAssocItem` error (from compiler/rustc_hir_analysis/src/errors.rs) with error code E0221 for types and E0222 for equality bindings.\\n\\n2. **Trait Selection Ambiguity**
